      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="D">D</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: D">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="k">import</span> <span class="n">std</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nb">string</span><span class="p">;</span>
<span class="k">import</span> <span class="n">std</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">algorithm</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="c1">// for min, already defines levenshteinDistance in library</span>

<span class="k">pure</span> <span class="k">nothrow</span> <span class="nb">size_t</span> <span class="n">damerauDistance</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="k">const</span> <span class="nb">string</span> <span class="n">source</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="k">const</span> <span class="nb">string</span> <span class="n">target</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
	<span class="k">immutable</span> <span class="k">auto</span> <span class="n">sourceLength</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">source</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">length</span><span class="p">;</span>
	<span class="k">immutable</span> <span class="k">auto</span> <span class="n">targetLength</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">target</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">length</span><span class="p">;</span>
	<span class="k">auto</span> <span class="n">distance</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="nb">size_t</span><span class="p">[][](</span><span class="n">sourceLength</span> <span class="p">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">targetLength</span><span class="p">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">);</span> 
	<span class="k">for</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">auto</span> <span class="n">iSource</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="n">iSource</span> <span class="p">&lt;=</span> <span class="n">sourceLength</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="p">++</span><span class="n">iSource</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
		<span class="n">distance</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iSource</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">iSource</span><span class="p">;</span>
	<span class="p">}</span>
	<span class="k">for</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">auto</span> <span class="n">iTarget</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="n">iTarget</span> <span class="p">&lt;=</span> <span class="n">targetLength</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="p">++</span><span class="n">iTarget</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
		<span class="n">distance</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">iTarget</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">iTarget</span><span class="p">;</span>
	<span class="p">}</span>

	<span class="k">for</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">auto</span> <span class="n">iSource</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="n">iSource</span> <span class="p">&lt;=</span> <span class="n">sourceLength</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="p">++</span><span class="n">iSource</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
		<span class="k">for</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">auto</span> <span class="n">iTarget</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="n">iTarget</span> <span class="p">&lt;=</span> <span class="n">targetLength</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="p">++</span><span class="n">iTarget</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
			<span class="k">auto</span> <span class="n">delete1</span> <span class="p">=</span>  <span class="n">distance</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iSource</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">iTarget</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span>
			<span class="k">auto</span> <span class="n">insert1</span> <span class="p">=</span>  <span class="n">distance</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iSource</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">iTarget</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span>
			<span class="nb">size_t</span> <span class="n">marginalCost</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">source</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iSource</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">==</span> <span class="n">target</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iTarget</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">?</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span>
			<span class="k">auto</span> <span class="n">substitute</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">distance</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iSource</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">iTarget</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">+</span> <span class="n">marginalCost</span><span class="p">;</span>
			<span class="n">distance</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iSource</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">iTarget</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">delete1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">insert1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">substitute</span><span class="p">);</span>
			<span class="k">if</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">iSource</span> <span class="p">&gt;</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="p">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="n">iTarget</span> <span class="p">&gt;</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="p">&amp;&amp;</span> 
				<span class="n">source</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iSource</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">==</span> <span class="n">target</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iTarget</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">&amp;&amp;</span>
				<span class="n">source</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iSource</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">==</span> <span class="n">target</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iTarget</span><span class="p">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">])</span> <span class="p">{</span>
					<span class="n">distance</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iSource</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">iTarget</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> 
						<span class="n">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">distance</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iSource</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">iTarget</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="n">distance</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">iSource</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">iTarget</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="mi">2</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">+</span> <span class="n">marginalCost</span><span class="p">);</span>
			<span class="p">}</span>
		<span class="p">}</span>
	<span class="p">}</span>
	<span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">distance</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">sourceLength</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">targetLength</span><span class="p">];</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre>
      </div> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Delphi">Delphi</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Delphi">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>A simple implementation that can certainly be improved upon.</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="k">function</span> <span class="nf">Levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Word1</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">Word2</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="k">String</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kt">integer</span><span class="o">;</span>
<span class="k">var</span> <span class="n">lev</span> <span class="o">:</span> <span class="k">array</span> <span class="k">of</span> <span class="k">array</span> <span class="k">of</span> <span class="kt">integer</span><span class="o">;</span>
    <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">,</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">:</span> <span class="kt">integer</span><span class="o">;</span>
<span class="k">begin</span>  
   <span class="c1">// Word1 := LowerCase(Word1);</span>
   <span class="c1">// Word2 := LowerCase(Word2);</span>

  <span class="c1">// If the words are identical, do nothing</span>
  <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">Word1</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Word2</span> <span class="k">then</span>
  <span class="k">begin</span>
    <span class="bp">result</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">;</span>
    <span class="k">exit</span><span class="o">;</span>
  <span class="k">end</span><span class="o">;</span>

  <span class="nb">SetLength</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="nb">length</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Word1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">;</span>
  <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="nb">low</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">to</span> <span class="nb">high</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">do</span>
    <span class="nb">setLength</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">]</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="nb">length</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Word2</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">;</span>

  <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="nb">low</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">to</span> <span class="nb">high</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">do</span> <span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">;</span>
  <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="nb">low</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nb">low</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">)])</span> <span class="k">to</span> <span class="nb">high</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nb">low</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">)])</span> <span class="k">do</span> <span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">;</span>

  <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="nb">low</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span> <span class="k">to</span> <span class="nb">high</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">do</span>
    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="nb">low</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">])</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span> <span class="k">to</span> <span class="nb">high</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">])</span> <span class="k">do</span>
      <span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="nb">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">,</span><span class="n">lev</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Eiffel">Eiffel</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Eiffel">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
	<span class="n">distance</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">b</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nc">STRING</span><span class="p">):</span> <span class="nc">INTEGER</span>
			<span class="c1">-- Compute Levenshtein distance between strings `a' and `b'.</span>
		<span class="kr">note</span>
			<span class="n">synopsis</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">"[</span>
<span class="s">				Example: Calculate distance between "sitting" and "kitten":</span>
<span class="s">				</span>
<span class="s">						k	i	t	t	e	n</span>
<span class="s">					0	1	2	3	4	5	6 &lt;-- set top row to [0 .. m]</span>
<span class="s">				s	1	1	2	3	4	5	6</span>
<span class="s">				i	2	2	1	2	3	4	5</span>
<span class="s">				t	3	3	2	1	2	3	4</span>
<span class="s">				t	4	4	3	2	1	2	3</span>
<span class="s">				i	5	5	4	3	2	2	3</span>
<span class="s">				n	6	6	5	4	3	3	2</span>
<span class="s">				g	7	7	6	5	4	4	3! &lt;-- Answer</span>
<span class="s">					^</span>
<span class="s">					|</span>
<span class="s">					set first column to [0 .. n]</span>
<span class="s">					</span>
<span class="s">				Compute top row and left-most columns first. Then go cell-by-cell</span>
<span class="s">				(e.g. 1 .. n over 1 .. m), row-by-row, column-by-column, computing:</span>
<span class="s">				</span>
<span class="s">				d[i-1, j] + 1		-- a deletion</span>
<span class="s">				d[i, j-1] + 1		-- an insertion</span>
<span class="s">				d[i-1, j-1] + 1		-- a substitution</span>
<span class="s">				</span>
<span class="s">				Taking the minimum of each and putting it in its proper place in</span>
<span class="s">				the d[i, j] array, unless the char's are the same (e.g. a [i - 1] = b [j - 1])</span>
<span class="s">				]"</span>
			<span class="n">language_note</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="s">"[</span>
<span class="s">				Eiffel is a 1-based array system and not 0-based, so do not</span>
<span class="s">				read the array element accesses from the 0-based mindset.</span>
<span class="s">				]"</span>
		<span class="kr">local</span>
			<span class="n">d</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nc">ARRAY2</span> <span class="o">[</span><span class="nc">INTEGER</span><span class="o">]</span>
			<span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">m</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">n</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nc">INTEGER</span>
		<span class="kr">do</span>
			<span class="n">m</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">a</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">count</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="n">n</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">b</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">count</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span>
			<span class="kr">create</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">make_filled</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">m</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">n</span><span class="p">)</span>
			<span class="kr">from</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="kr">until</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">m</span> <span class="kr">loop</span> <span class="n">d</span> <span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="kr">end</span>
			<span class="kr">from</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="kr">until</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">n</span> <span class="kr">loop</span> <span class="n">d</span> <span class="o">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="kr">end</span>
			<span class="kr">from</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="mi">2</span> <span class="kr">until</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="n">n</span> <span class="kr">loop</span>
				<span class="kr">from</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="mi">2</span> <span class="kr">until</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">&gt;</span> <span class="n">m</span> <span class="kr">loop</span>
					<span class="kr">if</span> <span class="n">a</span> <span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">b</span> <span class="o">[</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="kr">then</span>
						<span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span>
					<span class="kr">else</span>
						<span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">min</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">min</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span>
					<span class="kr">end</span>
					<span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span>
				<span class="kr">end</span>
				<span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span>
			<span class="kr">end</span>
			<span class="kc">Result</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">m</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">n</span><span class="o">]</span>
		<span class="kr">end</span>
</pre>
      </div> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Emacs_Lisp">Emacs Lisp</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Emacs Lisp">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
 <span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">defun</span> <span class="nv">levenshtein-distance</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">str1</span> <span class="nv">str2</span><span class="p">)</span>
   <span class="s">"Return the edit distance between strings STR1 and STR2."</span>
   <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">if</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">not</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">stringp</span> <span class="nv">str1</span><span class="p">))</span>
       <span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">error</span> <span class="s">"Argument was not a string: %s"</span> <span class="nv">str1</span><span class="p">))</span>
   <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">if</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">not</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">stringp</span> <span class="nv">str2</span><span class="p">))</span>
       <span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">error</span> <span class="s">"Argument was not a string: %s"</span> <span class="nv">str2</span><span class="p">))</span>
   <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">let*</span> <span class="p">((</span><span class="nv">make-table</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">function</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">lambda</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">columns</span> <span class="nv">rows</span> <span class="nv">init</span><span class="p">)</span>
            <span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">make-vector</span> <span class="nv">rows</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">make-vector</span> <span class="nv">columns</span> <span class="nv">init</span><span class="p">)))))</span>
          <span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">tref</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">function</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">lambda</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">table</span> <span class="nv">x</span> <span class="nv">y</span><span class="p">)</span>
            <span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">aref</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">aref</span> <span class="nv">table</span> <span class="nv">y</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="nv">x</span><span class="p">))))</span>
          <span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">tset</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">function</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">lambda</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">table</span> <span class="nv">x</span> <span class="nv">y</span> <span class="nv">object</span><span class="p">)</span>
            <span class="p">(</span><span class="k">let</span> <span class="p">((</span><span class="nv">row</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">copy-sequence</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nb">aref</span> <span class="nv">table</span> <span class="nv">y</span><span class="p">))))</span>
              <span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">aset</span> <span class="nv">row</span> <span class="nv">x</span> <span class="nv">object</span><span class="p">)</span>

      <p>and here's a slightly faster lazy version.</p>

       <pre>
<span class="k">let</span> <span class="nv">wagnerFischerLazy</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="n">s</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kt">string</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="n">t</span><span class="o">:</span> <span class="kt">string</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">=</span>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Go">Go</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Go">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>This version uses dynamic programming with time complexity of <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"> 
          <semantics> 
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"> 
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0"> 
             <mi>
              O
             </mi> 
             <mo stretchy="false">
              (
             </mo> 
             <mi>
              m
             </mi> 
             <mi>
              n
             </mi> 
             <mo stretchy="false">
              )
             </mo> 
            </mstyle> 
           </mrow> 
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle O(mn)}
           </annotation> 
          </semantics> 
         </math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/89ea09572a098b4762141a22c43a7ba1c20051cf" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:7.07ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="O(mn)"></span> where <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"> 
          <semantics> 
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"> 
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0"> 
             <mi>
              m
             </mi> 
            </mstyle> 
           </mrow> 
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle m}
           </annotation> 
          </semantics> 
         </math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a07d98bb302f3856cbabc47b2b9016692e3f7bc" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.051ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="m"></span> and <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"> 
          <semantics> 
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"> 
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0"> 
             <mi>
              n
             </mi> 
            </mstyle> 
           </mrow> 
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle n}
           </annotation> 
          </semantics> 
         </math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.405ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="n"></span> are lengths of <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"> 
          <semantics> 
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"> 
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0"> 
             <mi>
              a
             </mi> 
            </mstyle> 
           </mrow> 
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle a}
           </annotation> 
          </semantics> 
         </math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.24ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="a"></span> and <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"> 
          <semantics> 
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"> 
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0"> 
             <mi>
              b
             </mi> 
            </mstyle> 
           </mrow> 
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle b}
           </annotation> 
          </semantics> 
         </math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.008ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="b"></span>, and the space complexity is <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"> 
          <semantics> 
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"> 
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0"> 
             <mi>
              n
             </mi> 
             <mo>
              +
             </mo> 
             <mn>
              1
             </mn> 
            </mstyle> 
           </mrow> 
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle n+1}
           </annotation> 
          </semantics> 
         </math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2a135e65a42f2d73cccbfc4569523996ca0036f1" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:5.429ex; height:2.343ex;" alt="n+1"></span> of integers plus some constant space(i.e. <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"> 
          <semantics> 
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"> 
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0"> 
             <mi>
              O
             </mi> 
             <mo stretchy="false">
              (
             </mo> 
             <mi>
              n
             </mi> 
             <mo stretchy="false">
              )
             </mo> 
            </mstyle> 
           </mrow> 
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle O(n)}
           </annotation> 
          </semantics> 
         </math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/34109fe397fdcff370079185bfdb65826cb5565a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.019ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="O(n)"></span>).</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="kn">import</span> <span class="s">"unicode/utf8"</span>
<span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nx">Levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">a</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">b</span> <span class="kt">string</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kt">int</span> <span class="p">{</span>
	<span class="nx">f</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="nb">make</span><span class="p">([]</span><span class="kt">int</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">utf8</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">RuneCountInString</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">b</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span>

	<span class="k">for</span> <span class="nx">j</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="k">range</span> <span class="nx">f</span> <span class="p">{</span>
		<span class="nx">f</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nx">j</span>
	<span class="p">}</span>

	<span class="k">for</span> <span class="nx">_</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">ca</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="k">range</span> <span class="nx">a</span> <span class="p">{</span>
		<span class="nx">j</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="mi">1</span>
		<span class="nx">fj1</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="nx">f</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="c1">// fj1 is the value of f[j - 1] in last iteration</span>
		<span class="nx">f</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span><span class="o">++</span>
		<span class="k">for</span> <span class="nx">_</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">cb</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="k">range</span> <span class="nx">b</span> <span class="p">{</span>
			<span class="nx">mn</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="nx">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">f</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="p">]</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">f</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1">// delete &amp; insert</span>
			<span class="k">if</span> <span class="nx">cb</span> <span class="o">!=</span> <span class="nx">ca</span> <span class="p">{</span>
				<span class="nx">mn</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nx">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">mn</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">fj1</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1">// change</span>
			<span class="p">}</span> <span class="k">else</span> <span class="p">{</span>
				<span class="nx">mn</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nx">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">mn</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">fj1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="c1">// matched</span>
			<span class="p">}</span>

			<span class="nx">fj1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">f</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nx">f</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="nx">mn</span> <span class="c1">// save f[j] to fj1(j is about to increase), update f[j] to mn</span>
			<span class="nx">j</span><span class="o">++</span>
		<span class="p">}</span>
	<span class="p">}</span>

	<span class="k">return</span> <span class="nx">f</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nb">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">f</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
<span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nx">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">a</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">b</span> <span class="kt">int</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kt">int</span> <span class="p">{</span>
         <span class="k">if</span> <span class="nx">a</span> <span class="o">&lt;=</span> <span class="nx">b</span> <span class="p">{</span>
                 <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nx">a</span>
         <span class="p">}</span> <span class="k">else</span> <span class="p">{</span>
                 <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nx">b</span>
         <span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre>
      </div>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Haskell">Haskell</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Haskell">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<span class="nf">levenshtein</span> <span class="n">s</span> <span class="n">t</span> <span class="ow">=</span> 
    <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">!!</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">length</span> <span class="n">s</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">!!</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">length</span> <span class="n">t</span><span class="p">)</span> 
    <span class="kr">where</span> <span class="n">d</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="p">[[</span><span class="n">distance</span> <span class="n">m</span> <span class="n">n</span><span class="o">|</span><span class="n">n</span><span class="ow">&lt;-</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="n">length</span> <span class="n">t</span><span class="p">]]</span><span class="o">|</span><span class="n">m</span><span class="ow">&lt;-</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="n">length</span> <span class="n">s</span><span class="p">]]</span>

      <p>For large strings, using arrays is much faster</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="kr">import</span> <span class="nn">Data.Array.Unboxed</span>
<span class="kr">import</span> <span class="nn">Data.Array.ST</span>
<span class="kr">import</span> <span class="nn">Control.Monad.ST</span>

<span class="nf">for_</span> <span class="n">xs</span> <span class="n">f</span> <span class="ow">=</span>  <span class="n">mapM_</span> <span class="n">f</span> <span class="n">xs</span>

<span class="nf">levenshtein</span> <span class="ow">::</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="kt">Char</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="ow">-&gt;</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="kt">Char</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="ow">-&gt;</span> <span class="kt">Int</span>
<span class="nf">levenshtein</span> <span class="n">s</span> <span class="n">t</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">d</span> <span class="o">!</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">ls</span> <span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">lt</span><span class="p">)</span>
    <span class="kr">where</span> <span class="n">s'</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">array</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">ls</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">[</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">|</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="ow">&lt;-</span> <span class="n">zip</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="n">s</span> <span class="p">]</span><span class="ow">::</span><span class="kt">UArray</span> <span class="kt">Int</span> <span class="kt">Char</span>
          <span class="n">t'</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">array</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">lt</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">[</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">|</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="ow">&lt;-</span> <span class="n">zip</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="n">t</span> <span class="p">]</span><span class="ow">::</span><span class="kt">UArray</span> <span class="kt">Int</span> <span class="kt">Char</span>
          <span class="n">ls</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">length</span> <span class="n">s</span>
          <span class="n">lt</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">length</span> <span class="n">t</span>
          <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">l</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">h</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="p">((</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">),(</span><span class="n">length</span> <span class="n">s</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">length</span> <span class="n">t</span><span class="p">))</span>
          <span class="n">d</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">runSTUArray</span> <span class="o">$</span> <span class="kr">do</span>
                <span class="n">m</span> <span class="ow">&lt;-</span> <span class="n">newArray</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">l</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">h</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="ow">::</span> <span class="kt">ST</span> <span class="n">s</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="kt">STUArray</span> <span class="n">s</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="kt">Int</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="kt">Int</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="kt">Int</span><span class="p">)</span>
                <span class="n">for_</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="n">ls</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">$</span> <span class="nf">\</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="ow">-&gt;</span> <span class="n">writeArray</span> <span class="n">m</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="n">i</span>
                <span class="n">for_</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="n">lt</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">$</span> <span class="nf">\</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="ow">-&gt;</span> <span class="n">writeArray</span> <span class="n">m</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="n">j</span>
                <span class="n">for_</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="n">lt</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">$</span> <span class="nf">\</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="ow">-&gt;</span> <span class="kr">do</span>
                              <span class="n">for_</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="n">ls</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">$</span> <span class="nf">\</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="ow">-&gt;</span> <span class="kr">do</span>

                <span class="n">return</span> <span class="n">m</span>

      </div> 
      <p>As recursively defined array:</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>

<span class="nf">toArray</span> <span class="n">l</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">listArray</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">length</span> <span class="n">l</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="n">l</span>                  <span class="c1">-- makes an Array from a List</span>
<span class="nf">mkArray</span> <span class="n">f</span> <span class="n">bnds</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">array</span> <span class="n">bnds</span> <span class="p">[</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">f</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">|</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="ow">&lt;-</span> <span class="n">range</span> <span class="n">bnds</span> <span class="p">]</span> <span class="c1">-- defines an Array over its indices</span>

<span class="nf">levenshtein</span> <span class="n">sa</span> <span class="n">sb</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">table</span>
  <span class="kr">where</span>
    <span class="n">arrA</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">toArray</span> <span class="n">sa</span>

    <span class="n">f</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">ia</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">ia</span>
    <span class="n">f</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span> <span class="p">,</span><span class="n">ib</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">ib</span>

      <p>And finally: fast but cryptic implementation</p>

<span class="nf">levenshtein2</span> <span class="n">sa</span> <span class="n">sb</span> <span class="ow">=</span> <span class="n">last</span> <span class="o">$</span> <span class="n">foldl</span> <span class="n">transform</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="n">length</span> <span class="n">sa</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="n">sb</span>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Io">Io</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Io">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
 <span class="n">Levenshtein</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="k">method</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">left</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">right</span><span class="o">,</span>
   <span class="k">if</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">right</span> <span class="n">size</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="n">left</span> <span class="n">size</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">return</span> <span class="n">Levenshtein</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">right</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">left</span><span class="o">))</span>
   <span class="n">current</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="mf">0</span> <span class="n">to</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">left</span> <span class="n">size</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="n">asList</span>
   <span class="n">right</span> <span class="n">foreach</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">righti</span><span class="o">,</span>
     <span class="n">previous</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="n">current</span>

     <span class="n">left</span> <span class="n">foreach</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">leftj</span><span class="o">,</span>
       <span class="n">current</span> <span class="n">append</span><span class="o">((</span><span class="n">current</span> <span class="n">at</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mf">1</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="n">min</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">previous</span> <span class="n">at</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mf">1</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mf">1</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="n">min</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">previous</span> <span class="n">at</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="k">if</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">leftj</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="n">righti</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="mf">0</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="mf">1</span><span class="o">)))</span>

   <span class="n">current</span> <span class="n">last</span>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="JavaScript">JavaScript</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: JavaScript">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>Slow recursive version:</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="kd">function</span> <span class="nx">levenshteinDistance</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">s</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">t</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
        <span class="k">if</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">s</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span> <span class="o">===</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nx">t</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span><span class="p">;</span>
        <span class="k">if</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">t</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span> <span class="o">===</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nx">s</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span><span class="p">;</span>

        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nb">Math</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">min</span><span class="p">(</span>
                <span class="nx">levenshteinDistance</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">s</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">substr</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="nx">t</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
                <span class="nx">levenshteinDistance</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">t</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">substr</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="nx">s</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
                <span class="nx">levenshteinDistance</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">s</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">substr</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="nx">t</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">substr</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">s</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">!==</span> <span class="nx">t</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">?</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="o">:</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="p">);</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre>
      </div> 
      <p>Faster approach using dynamic programming</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="c1">// Compute the edit distance between the two given strings</span>
<span class="kd">function</span> <span class="nx">getEditDistance</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">a</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">b</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
  <span class="k">if</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">a</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span> <span class="o">===</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nx">b</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span><span class="p">;</span> 
  <span class="k">if</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">b</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span> <span class="o">===</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nx">a</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span><span class="p">;</span>

  <span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nx">matrix</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[];</span>

  <span class="c1">// increment along the first column of each row</span>
  <span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nx">i</span><span class="p">;</span>
  <span class="k">for</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nx">i</span> <span class="o">&lt;=</span> <span class="nx">b</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nx">i</span><span class="o">++</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
    <span class="nx">matrix</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">i</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">i</span><span class="p">];</span>
  <span class="p">}</span>

  <span class="c1">// increment each column in the first row</span>
  <span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nx">j</span><span class="p">;</span>
  <span class="k">for</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">j</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nx">j</span> <span class="o">&lt;=</span> <span class="nx">a</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nx">j</span><span class="o">++</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
    <span class="nx">matrix</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nx">j</span><span class="p">;</span>
  <span class="p">}</span>

  <span class="c1">// Fill in the rest of the matrix</span>
  <span class="k">for</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nx">i</span> <span class="o">&lt;=</span> <span class="nx">b</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nx">i</span><span class="o">++</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">j</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nx">j</span> <span class="o">&lt;=</span> <span class="nx">a</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span><span class="p">;</span> <span class="nx">j</span><span class="o">++</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
      <span class="k">if</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">b</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">charAt</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="nx">a</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">charAt</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">))</span> <span class="p">{</span>
        <span class="nx">matrix</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">i</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nx">matrix</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">];</span>
      <span class="p">}</span> <span class="k">else</span> <span class="p">{</span>
        <span class="nx">matrix</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">i</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">Math</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">matrix</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="c1">// substitution</span>
                                <span class="nb">Math</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">matrix</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">i</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="c1">// insertion</span>
                                         <span class="nx">matrix</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="nx">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">));</span> <span class="c1">// deletion</span>
      <span class="p">}</span>
    <span class="p">}</span>
  <span class="p">}</span>

  <span class="k">return</span> <span class="nx">matrix</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">b</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span><span class="p">][</span><span class="nx">a</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">length</span><span class="p">];</span>
<span class="p">};</span>
</pre>
      </div>

        <span class="kt">int</span><span class="o">[][]</span> <span class="n">distance</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="kt">int</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">lhs</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="na">length</span><span class="o">()</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">rhs</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="na">length</span><span class="o">()</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">];</span>        
                                                                                 
        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="kt">int</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">;</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">&lt;=</span> <span class="n">lhs</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="na">length</span><span class="o">();</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">++)</span>

      <p>Not recursive and faster</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="kd">public</span> <span class="kt">int</span> <span class="nf">levenshteinDistance</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="n">CharSequence</span> <span class="n">lhs</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">CharSequence</span> <span class="n">rhs</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">{</span>                          
    <span class="kt">int</span> <span class="n">len0</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">lhs</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="na">length</span><span class="o">()</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">;</span>                                                     
    <span class="kt">int</span> <span class="n">len1</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">rhs</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="na">length</span><span class="o">()</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">;</span>                                                     
                                                                                    
    <span class="c1">// the array of distances                                                       </span>
    <span class="kt">int</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">cost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="kt">int</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">len0</span><span class="o">];</span>                                                     
    <span class="kt">int</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">newcost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="k">new</span> <span class="kt">int</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">len0</span><span class="o">];</span>                                                  
                                                                                    
    <span class="c1">// initial cost of skipping prefix in String s0                                 </span>
    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="kt">int</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">;</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="n">len0</span><span class="o">;</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">++)</span> <span class="n">cost</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">;</span>                                     
                                                                                    
    <span class="c1">// dynamically computing the array of distances                                  </span>
                                                                                    
    <span class="c1">// transformation cost for each letter in s1                                    </span>
    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="kt">int</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">;</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="n">len1</span><span class="o">;</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">++)</span> <span class="o">{</span>                                                
        <span class="c1">// initial cost of skipping prefix in String s1                             </span>
        <span class="n">newcost</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">;</span>                                                             
                                                                                    
        <span class="c1">// transformation cost for each letter in s0                                </span>
        <span class="k">for</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="kt">int</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">;</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="n">len0</span><span class="o">;</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">++)</span> <span class="o">{</span>                                             
            <span class="c1">// matching current letters in both strings                             </span>
            <span class="kt">int</span> <span class="n">match</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="n">lhs</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="na">charAt</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="n">rhs</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="na">charAt</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">))</span> <span class="o">?</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="o">:</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">;</span>             
                                                                                    
            <span class="c1">// computing cost for each transformation                               </span>
            <span class="kt">int</span> <span class="n">cost_replace</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">cost</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">match</span><span class="o">;</span>                                 
            <span class="kt">int</span> <span class="n">cost_insert</span>  <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">cost</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">;</span>                                         
            <span class="kt">int</span> <span class="n">cost_delete</span>  <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">newcost</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">;</span>                                  
                                                                                    
            <span class="c1">// keep minimum cost                                                    </span>
            <span class="n">newcost</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Math</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="na">min</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">Math</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="na">min</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">cost_insert</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">cost_delete</span><span class="o">),</span> <span class="n">cost_replace</span><span class="o">);</span>
        <span class="o">}</span>                                                                           
                                                                                    
        <span class="c1">// swap cost/newcost arrays                                                 </span>
        <span class="kt">int</span><span class="o">[]</span> <span class="n">swap</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">cost</span><span class="o">;</span> <span class="n">cost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">newcost</span><span class="o">;</span> <span class="n">newcost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">swap</span><span class="o">;</span>                          
    <span class="o">}</span>                                                                               
                                                                                    
    <span class="c1">// the distance is the cost for transforming all letters in both strings        </span>
    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">cost</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">len0</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">];</span>                                                          
<span class="o">}</span>
</pre>
      </div> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Julia">Julia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Julia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>Straightforward recursive implementation. Do not use for large strings!</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="k">function</span> <span class="n">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lhs</span><span class="o">::</span><span class="n">String</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rhs</span><span class="o">::</span><span class="n">String</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">lhsi</span><span class="o">::</span><span class="kt">Int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">length</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lhs</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="n">rhsi</span><span class="o">::</span><span class="kt">Int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">length</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">rhs</span><span class="p">))</span>
    <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">lhsi</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">rhsi</span>
    <span class="k">end</span>
    <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">rhsi</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">lhsi</span>
    <span class="k">end</span>

    <span class="n">cost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">lhs</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">lhsi</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="n">rhs</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">rhsi</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">?</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="o">:</span> <span class="mi">1</span>
    <span class="n">min</span><span class="p">(</span>
        <span class="n">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lhs</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rhs</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">lhsi</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rhsi</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
        <span class="n">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lhs</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rhs</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">lhsi</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rhsi</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
        <span class="n">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lhs</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rhs</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">lhsi</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rhsi</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">cost</span>
        <span class="p">)</span>
<span class="k">end</span>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Kotlin">Kotlin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Kotlin">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="k">fun</span> <span class="nf">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lhs</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">CharSequence</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rhs</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">CharSequence</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Int</span> <span class="p">{</span>
    <span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">lhsLength</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">lhs</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">length</span>
    <span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">rhsLength</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">rhs</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">length</span>

    <span class="k">var</span> <span class="py">cost</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">Array</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lhsLength</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="n">it</span> <span class="p">}</span>
    <span class="k">var</span> <span class="py">newCost</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">Array</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lhsLength</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="m">0</span> <span class="p">}</span>

    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="k">in</span> <span class="m">1.</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">rhsLength</span><span class="p">-</span><span class="m">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
        <span class="n">newCost</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="m">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">i</span>

        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="k">in</span> <span class="m">1.</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">lhsLength</span><span class="p">-</span><span class="m">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
            <span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">match</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="k">if</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">lhs</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="m">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">==</span> <span class="n">rhs</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="m">1</span><span class="p">])</span> <span class="m">0</span> <span class="k">else</span> <span class="m">1</span>

            <span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">costReplace</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">cost</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="m">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">+</span> <span class="n">match</span>
            <span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">costInsert</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">cost</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">+</span> <span class="m">1</span>
            <span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">costDelete</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">newCost</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="m">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">+</span> <span class="m">1</span>

            <span class="n">newCost</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">Math</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Math</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">costInsert</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">costDelete</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="n">costReplace</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="p">}</span>

        <span class="k">val</span> <span class="py">swap</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">cost</span>
        <span class="n">cost</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">newCost</span>
        <span class="n">newCost</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">swap</span>
    <span class="p">}</span>

    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">cost</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">lhsLength</span> <span class="p">-</span> <span class="m">1</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre>
      </div> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="MySQL">MySQL</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: MySQL">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>This implementation seems to be broken; but I am not entirely sure how to fix it.</p>

<span class="k">CREATE</span> <span class="n">FUNCTION</span> <span class="ss">`levenshtein`</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="ss">`s1`</span> <span class="kt">VARCHAR</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">255</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">CHARACTER</span> <span class="kt">SET</span> <span class="n">utf8</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="ss">`s2`</span> <span class="kt">VARCHAR</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">255</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">CHARACTER</span> <span class="kt">SET</span> <span class="n">utf8</span><span class="p">)</span>

    <span class="c1">-- max strlen=255 for this function</span>
    <span class="k">DECLARE</span> <span class="n">cv0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">cv1</span> <span class="kt">VARBINARY</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">256</span><span class="p">);</span>
    
    <span class="c1">-- if any param is NULL return NULL</span>
    <span class="c1">-- (consistent with builtin functions)</span>
    <span class="k">IF</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">s1</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">s2</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">IS</span> <span class="no">NULL</span> <span class="k">THEN</span>
