      <p>"(Note) this is just one of many implementations of the Levenshtein Distance, but I've not been able to get the others to work</p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="rexx">rexx</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: rexx">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="cm">/* rexx levenshtein calculates the edit distance   Karlocai 2009-01-18</span>
<span class="cm">    between 2 strings s and t</span>

<span class="cm">   This implementation of the Levenshtein algorithm </span>
<span class="cm">   uses one row only (0..n), containing </span>
<span class="cm">   - values of the previous line in columns [i-1]..n and </span>
<span class="cm">   - values of the current  line in columns 1..[i-2]</span>
<span class="cm">   The current left value is kept in the variable lc</span>
<span class="cm">   i: column 1..n of s, 1st index</span>
<span class="cm">   j: row    1..m of t, 2nd index</span>
<span class="cm">*/</span>

<span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">Parse</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">Arg</span><span class="w"> </span>s<span class="o">,</span>t<span class="w">                </span><span class="o">--</span><span class="w"> </span>gets<span class="w"> </span><span class="m">2</span><span class="w"> </span>strings<span class="w"> </span>as<span class="w"> </span>parameter

<span class="w"> </span>n<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nb">Length</span><span class="o">(</span>s<span class="o">)</span><span class="w">                </span><span class="o">--</span><span class="w"> </span>checks<span class="w"> </span>the<span class="w"> </span>parameters
<span class="w"> </span>m<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nb">Length</span><span class="o">(</span>t<span class="o">)</span>
<span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">If</span><span class="w"> </span>n<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="m">0</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">Then</span>
<span class="w">   </span><span class="kr">Return</span><span class="w"> </span>m
<span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">If</span><span class="w"> </span>m<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="m">0</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">Then</span>
<span class="w">   </span><span class="kr">Return</span><span class="w"> </span>n

<span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">Do</span><span class="w"> </span>i<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="m">0</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">To</span><span class="w"> </span>n<span class="w">                </span><span class="o">--</span><span class="w"> </span>initializes<span class="w"> </span>the<span class="w"> </span><span class="m">1</span>st<span class="w"> </span>row
<span class="w">   </span>r<span class="o">.</span>i<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span>i
<span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">End</span>

<span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">Do</span><span class="w"> </span>j<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="m">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">To</span><span class="w"> </span>m<span class="w">                </span><span class="o">--</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">for</span><span class="w"> </span>each<span class="w"> </span>row
<span class="w">   </span>lc<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span>j<span class="w">                     </span><span class="o">--</span><span class="w"> </span>left<span class="w"> </span>column<span class="w"> </span>start<span class="w"> </span>value
<span class="w">   </span><span class="kr">Do</span><span class="w"> </span>i<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="m">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">To</span><span class="w"> </span>n<span class="w">              </span><span class="o">--</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">for</span><span class="w"> </span>each<span class="w"> </span>column
<span class="w">     </span>nv<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nb">Min</span><span class="o">(</span>r<span class="o">.</span>i<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">+</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="m">1</span><span class="o">,</span><span class="w">   </span><span class="o">,</span>
<span class="w">              </span>lc<span class="w">  </span><span class="o">+</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="m">1</span><span class="o">,</span><span class="w">   </span><span class="o">,</span>
<span class="w">              </span>r<span class="o">.</span><span class="err">[</span>i<span class="o">-</span><span class="m">1</span><span class="err">]</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">+</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">(</span><span class="nb">Substr</span><span class="o">(</span>s<span class="o">,</span>i<span class="o">,</span><span class="m">1</span><span class="o">)</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">&lt;&gt;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nb">Substr</span><span class="o">(</span>t<span class="o">,</span>j<span class="o">,</span><span class="m">1</span><span class="o">)))</span><span class="w">  </span>
<span class="w">     </span>r<span class="o">.</span><span class="err">[</span>i<span class="o">-</span><span class="m">1</span><span class="err">]</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span>lc<span class="w">             </span><span class="o">--</span><span class="w"> </span>sets<span class="w"> </span>previous<span class="w"> </span>left<span class="w"> </span>column
<span class="w">     </span>lc<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span>nv<span class="w">                  </span><span class="o">--</span><span class="w"> </span>current<span class="w"> </span>left<span class="w"> </span>column
<span class="w">   </span><span class="kr">End</span>
<span class="w">   </span>r<span class="o">.</span>n<span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span>lc<span class="w">                   </span><span class="o">--</span><span class="w"> </span>sets<span class="w"> </span>last<span class="w"> </span>current<span class="w"> </span>value
<span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">End</span>
<span class="w"> </span><span class="kr">Return</span><span class="w"> </span>r<span class="o">.</span>n
</pre>
      </div> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ruby">Ruby</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Ruby">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>This Ruby version is simple, but extremely slow, though it works with any Array with elements that implement '=='.</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="ss">first</span><span class="p">:,</span> <span class="ss">second</span><span class="p">:)</span>
  <span class="k">case</span>
    <span class="k">when</span> <span class="n">first</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">empty?</span> <span class="k">then</span> <span class="n">second</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span>
    <span class="k">when</span> <span class="n">second</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">empty?</span> <span class="k">then</span> <span class="n">first</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span>
    <span class="k">else</span> <span class="o">[</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">first</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="n">second</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="p">?</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="ss">first</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">first</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">..-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="ss">second</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">second</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">..-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span><span class="p">),</span>
          <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="ss">first</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">first</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">..-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="ss">second</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">second</span><span class="p">),</span>
          <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="ss">first</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">first</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="ss">second</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">second</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">..-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">].</span><span class="n">min</span>
  <span class="k">end</span>
<span class="k">end</span>
</pre>
      </div> 
      <p>This memoized version is significantly faster</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="ss">first</span><span class="p">:,</span> <span class="ss">second</span><span class="p">:)</span>
  <span class="n">matrix</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="o">[</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="n">first</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">to_a</span><span class="o">]</span>
  <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="n">second</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">each</span> <span class="k">do</span> <span class="o">|</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">|</span>
    <span class="n">matrix</span> <span class="o">&lt;&lt;</span> <span class="o">[</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="o">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">first</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span><span class="p">)</span>
  <span class="k">end</span>

  <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="n">second</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">each</span> <span class="k">do</span> <span class="o">|</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">|</span>
    <span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">..</span><span class="n">first</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">each</span> <span class="k">do</span> <span class="o">|</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">|</span>
      <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">first</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="n">second</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span>
        <span class="n">matrix</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">matrix</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span>
      <span class="k">else</span>
        <span class="n">matrix</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="o">[</span>
          <span class="n">matrix</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">]</span><span class="p">,</span>
          <span class="n">matrix</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span><span class="p">,</span>
          <span class="n">matrix</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span><span class="p">,</span>
        <span class="o">].</span><span class="n">min</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span>
      <span class="k">end</span>
    <span class="k">end</span>
  <span class="k">end</span>
  <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">matrix</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">last</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">last</span>
<span class="k">end</span>
</pre>
      </div> 
      <p>And another memoized version</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="ss">first</span><span class="p">:,</span> <span class="ss">second</span><span class="p">:)</span>
  <span class="n">m</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">n</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">first</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">second</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span>
  <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">m</span> <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">n</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
  <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">n</span> <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">m</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="mi">0</span>

  <span class="c1"># Create our distance matrix</span>
  <span class="n">d</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">Array</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">new</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">m</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="nb">Array</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">new</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">n</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)}</span>
  <span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">upto</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">m</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="o">|</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">|</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="p">}</span>
  <span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">upto</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">n</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span> <span class="o">|</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">|</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="p">}</span>

  <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">upto</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">n</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">do</span> <span class="o">|</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">|</span>
    <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">upto</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">m</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">do</span> <span class="o">|</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">|</span>
      <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">first</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="n">second</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="p">?</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="o">[</span><span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">]+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">]+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="o">].</span><span class="n">min</span>
    <span class="k">end</span>
  <span class="k">end</span>
  <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="n">m</span><span class="o">][</span><span class="n">n</span><span class="o">]</span>
<span class="k">end</span>
</pre>
      </div> 
      <p>A faster implementation for the Levenshtein distance of strings (using C bindings) is available <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://github.com/dbalatero/levenshtein-ffi">here</a></p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Rust">Rust</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Rust">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>A simple implementation in Rust (beta2), transposed from the C version. It is a little more general than the bare minimum, in fact it accepts any type that can be converted to a string.</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="k">fn</span> <span class="nf">levenshtein_d1stance</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">T</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">s1</span>: <span class="kp">&amp;</span><span class="nc">T</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">s2</span>: <span class="kp">&amp;</span><span class="nc">T</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span>-&gt; <span class="kt">usize</span> <span class="nc">where</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">T</span>: <span class="nb">ToString</span> <span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="kd">let</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v1</span>: <span class="nb">Vec</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">char</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">s1</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">to_string</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">chars</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">collect</span><span class="p">();</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="kd">let</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v2</span>: <span class="nb">Vec</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">char</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">s2</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">to_string</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">chars</span><span class="p">().</span><span class="n">collect</span><span class="p">();</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="kd">let</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v1len</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v1</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">len</span><span class="p">();</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="kd">let</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v2len</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v2</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">len</span><span class="p">();</span>
<span class="w">    </span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="c1">// Early exit if one of the strings is empty</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="k">if</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v1len</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">==</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="k">return</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v2len</span><span class="p">;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="k">if</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v2len</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">==</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="k">return</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v1len</span><span class="p">;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span>

<span class="w">    </span><span class="k">fn</span> <span class="nf">min3</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="n">T</span>: <span class="nb">Ord</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">v1</span>: <span class="nc">T</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v2</span>: <span class="nc">T</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v3</span>: <span class="nc">T</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span>-&gt; <span class="nc">T</span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="n">cmp</span>::<span class="n">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">v1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">cmp</span>::<span class="n">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">v2</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v3</span><span class="p">))</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="k">fn</span> <span class="nf">delta</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">x</span>: <span class="nc">char</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">y</span>: <span class="nc">char</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="w"> </span>-&gt; <span class="kt">usize</span> <span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="k">if</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">==</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">y</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="k">else</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="kd">let</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="k">mut</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">column</span>: <span class="nb">Vec</span><span class="o">&lt;</span><span class="kt">usize</span><span class="o">&gt;</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">..</span><span class="n">v1len</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">collect</span><span class="p">();</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="k">for</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="k">in</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">..</span><span class="n">v2len</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>

<span class="w">        </span><span class="kd">let</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="k">mut</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">lastdiag</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">x</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">;</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="k">for</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">y</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="k">in</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">..</span><span class="n">v1len</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="kd">let</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">olddiag</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">column</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">y</span><span class="p">];</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="n">column</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">y</span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">min3</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">column</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">y</span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">+</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                             </span><span class="n">column</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">y</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">+</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                             </span><span class="n">lastdiag</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">+</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">delta</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">v1</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">y</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">],</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">v2</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">x</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]));</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="n">lastdiag</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="o">=</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="n">olddiag</span><span class="p">;</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>

      </div> 
      <p>You can test it live on <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://slug.it/levenshtein-distance-rust">Rust Playpen</a>.</p> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Scala">Scala</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Scala">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>Imperative version. A functional version would likely be far more concise.</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="k">def</span> <span class="n">levenshtein</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">str1</span><span class="k">:</span> <span class="kt">String</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">str2</span><span class="k">:</span> <span class="kt">String</span><span class="o">)</span><span class="k">:</span> <span class="kt">Int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="o">{</span>
    <span class="k">val</span> <span class="n">lenStr1</span> <span class="k">=</span> <span class="n">str1</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span>
    <span class="k">val</span> <span class="n">lenStr2</span> <span class="k">=</span> <span class="n">str2</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span>

    <span class="k">val</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="k">:</span> <span class="kt">Array</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="kt">Array</span><span class="o">[</span><span class="kt">Int</span><span class="o">]]</span> <span class="k">=</span> <span class="nc">Array</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">ofDim</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">lenStr1</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">lenStr2</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">)</span>

    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="k">&lt;-</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="n">to</span> <span class="n">lenStr1</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">)(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="k">=</span> <span class="n">i</span>
    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="k">&lt;-</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="n">to</span> <span class="n">lenStr2</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">)(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="k">=</span> <span class="n">j</span>

    <span class="k">for</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="k">&lt;-</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="n">to</span> <span class="n">lenStr1</span><span class="o">;</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="k">&lt;-</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="n">to</span> <span class="n">lenStr2</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">{</span>
      <span class="k">val</span> <span class="n">cost</span> <span class="k">=</span> <span class="k">if</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="n">str1</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="n">str2</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">))</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="k">else</span> <span class="mi">1</span>

      <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">)(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="k">=</span> <span class="n">min</span><span class="o">(</span>
        <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">)(</span><span class="n">j</span>  <span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">,</span>     <span class="c1">// deletion</span>
        <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span>  <span class="o">)(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">,</span>     <span class="c1">// insertion</span>
        <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">)(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">cost</span>   <span class="c1">// substitution</span>
      <span class="o">)</span>
    <span class="o">}</span>

    <span class="n">d</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">lenStr1</span><span class="o">)(</span><span class="n">lenStr2</span><span class="o">)</span>
  <span class="o">}</span>

  <span class="k">def</span> <span class="n">min</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">nums</span><span class="k">:</span> <span class="kt">Int*</span><span class="o">)</span><span class="k">:</span> <span class="kt">Int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">nums</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">min</span>

      <p>Functional version.</p>

       <pre>
<span class="k">import</span> <span class="nn">scalaz.Memo</span>

<span class="k">def</span> <span class="n">levenshtein</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">s1</span><span class="k">:</span> <span class="kt">String</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">s2</span><span class="k">:</span> <span class="kt">String</span><span class="o">)</span><span class="k">:</span> <span class="kt">Int</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="o">{</span>
  <span class="k">lazy</span> <span class="k">val</span> <span class="n">lev</span><span class="k">:</span> <span class="o">((</span><span class="kt">Int</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="kt">Int</span><span class="o">))</span> <span class="k">=&gt;</span> <span class="nc">Int</span> <span class="k">=</span> <span class="nc">Memo</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">mutableHashMapMemo</span><span class="o">[(</span><span class="kt">Int</span>, <span class="kt">Int</span><span class="o">)</span>, <span class="kt">Int</span><span class="o">]</span> <span class="o">{</span>
    <span class="k">case</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="k">=&gt;</span> <span class="n">i</span>
    <span class="k">case</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="k">=&gt;</span> <span class="n">j</span>
    <span class="k">case</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="k">=&gt;</span> <span class="nc">Seq</span><span class="o">(</span>
      <span class="n">lev</span><span class="o">((</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">))</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">,</span>
      <span class="n">lev</span><span class="o">((</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">))</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">,</span>
      <span class="n">lev</span><span class="o">((</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">))</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="k">if</span> <span class="o">(</span><span class="n">s1</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">)</span> <span class="o">==</span> <span class="n">s2</span><span class="o">(</span><span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">))</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="k">else</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="o">)).</span><span class="n">min</span>
  <span class="o">}</span>
  <span class="n">lev</span><span class="o">((</span><span class="n">s1</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span><span class="o">,</span> <span class="n">s2</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">length</span><span class="o">))</span>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Smalltalk">Smalltalk</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Smalltalk">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="nf">levenshteinDistanceBetween:</span> <span class="nv">stringOne</span> <span class="nf">and:</span> <span class="nv">stringTwo</span> 
	
	<span class="c">"Iterative calculation of the Levenshtein distance between two strings."</span>
	
	<span class="o">|</span><span class="nv"> arrayTwo arrayOne</span><span class="o">|</span>
	<span class="c">" degenerate cases"</span>
	<span class="nv">stringTwo</span> <span class="nf">=</span> <span class="nv">stringOne</span> 
		<span class="nb">ifTrue:</span>[<span class="o">^</span><span class="m">0</span>]<span class="p">.</span>
	(<span class="nv">stringTwo</span> <span class="nf">size</span>) <span class="nf">=</span> <span class="m">0</span> 
		<span class="nb">ifTrue:</span>[<span class="o">^</span>(<span class="nv">stringOne</span> <span class="nf">size</span>)]<span class="p">.</span>
	(<span class="nv">stringOne</span> <span class="nf">size</span>) <span class="nf">=</span> <span class="m">0</span> 
		<span class="nb">ifTrue:</span>[<span class="o">^</span>(<span class="nv">stringTwo</span> <span class="nf">size</span>)]<span class="p">.</span>
	
	<span class="c">"create two work vectors of integer distances"</span>
	<span class="nv">arrayOne</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="nc">Array</span> <span class="nf">new:</span>((<span class="nv">stringTwo</span> <span class="nf">size</span>) <span class="nf">+</span> <span class="m">1</span>)<span class="p">.</span>
	<span class="nv">arrayTwo</span> <span class="o">:=</span> <span class="nc">Array</span> <span class="nf">new:</span>((<span class="nv">stringTwo</span> <span class="nf">size</span>) <span class="nf">+</span> <span class="m">1</span>)<span class="p">.</span>
	
	<span class="c">"initialize v0 (the previous row of distances)</span>
<span class="c">    	this row is A[0][i]: edit distance for an empty s</span>
<span class="c">    	the distance is just the number of characters to delete from t"</span>
	(<span class="m">1</span> <span class="nf">to:</span> (<span class="nv">arrayOne</span> <span class="nf">size</span>)) <span class="nf">do:</span>[ <span class="o">:</span><span class="nv">i</span> <span class="o">|</span> <span class="nv">arrayOne</span> <span class="nf">at:</span> <span class="nv">i</span> <span class="nf">put:</span> <span class="nv">i</span><span class="nf">-</span><span class="m">1</span> ]<span class="p">.</span>
	
	(<span class="m">1</span> <span class="nf">to:</span> (<span class="nv">stringOne</span> <span class="nf">size</span>)) <span class="nf">do:</span> [ <span class="o">:</span> <span class="nv">i</span> <span class="o">|</span> 	
		<span class="c">" calculate v1 (current row distances) from the previous row v0</span>
<span class="c">		first element of v1 is A[i+1][0] edit distance is delete (i+1) chars from s to match empty t"</span>
  		<span class="nv">arrayTwo</span> <span class="nf">at:</span> <span class="m">1</span> <span class="nf">put:</span> <span class="nv">i</span><span class="p">.</span>
		
		 <span class="c">" use formula to fill in the rest of the row"</span>
		(<span class="m">1</span> <span class="nf">to:</span> (<span class="nv">stringTwo</span> <span class="nf">size</span>)) <span class="nf">do:</span> [ <span class="o">:</span><span class="nv">j</span> <span class="o">||</span><span class="nv"> cost minimum minimumAux </span><span class="o">|</span>
			((<span class="nv">stringOne</span> <span class="nf">at:</span> <span class="nv">i</span>) <span class="nf">=</span> (<span class="nv">stringTwo</span> <span class="nf">at:</span> <span class="nv">j</span>)) 
				<span class="nb">ifTrue:</span>[<span class="err">cost</span><span class="o">:=</span><span class="m">0</span>]
				<span class="nb">ifFalse:</span>[<span class="err">cost</span><span class="o">:=</span><span class="m">1</span>]<span class="p">.</span>			
			<span class="nv">minimumAux</span> <span class="o">:=</span> ((<span class="nv">arrayTwo</span> <span class="nf">at:</span> <span class="nv">j</span>) <span class="nf">+</span> <span class="m">1</span>) <span class="nf">min:</span> ((<span class="nv">arrayOne</span> <span class="nf">at:</span> (<span class="nv">j</span><span class="nf">+</span><span class="m">1</span>)) <span class="nf">+</span> <span class="m">1</span>)<span class="p">.</span>
			<span class="nv">minimum</span> <span class="o">:=</span>  <span class="nv">minimumAux</span> <span class="nf">min:</span> ((<span class="nv">arrayOne</span> <span class="nf">at:</span> <span class="nv">j</span>) <span class="nf">+</span> <span class="nv">cost</span>)<span class="p">.</span>
			<span class="nv">arrayTwo</span> <span class="nf">at:</span> (<span class="nv">j</span><span class="nf">+</span><span class="m">1</span>) <span class="nf">put:</span> <span class="nv">minimum</span><span class="p">.</span>]<span class="p">.</span>
		
		(<span class="m">1</span> <span class="nf">to:</span> (<span class="nv">arrayOne</span> <span class="nf">size</span>)) <span class="nf">do:</span> [ <span class="o">:</span><span class="nv">j</span> <span class="o">|</span> <span class="nv">arrayOne</span> <span class="nf">at:</span> <span class="nv">j</span> <span class="nf">put:</span> (<span class="nv">arrayTwo</span> <span class="nf">at:</span> <span class="nv">j</span>) ]<span class="p">.</span>
		
		]<span class="p">.</span>

	<span class="o">^</span><span class="nv">arrayTwo</span> <span class="nf">at:</span> ((<span class="nv">stringTwo</span> <span class="nf">size</span>)<span class="nf">+</span><span class="m">1</span>)<span class="p">.</span>
</pre>
      </div> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Swift">Swift</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Swift">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="cm">/**</span>
<span class="cm"> * Levenshtein edit distance calculator</span>
<span class="cm"> *</span>
<span class="cm"> * Inspired by https://gist.github.com/bgreenlee/52d93a1d8fa1b8c1f38b</span>
<span class="cm"> * Improved with http://stackoverflow.com/questions/26990394/slow-swift-arrays-and-strings-performance</span>
<span class="cm"> */</span>

<span class="kd">class</span> <span class="nc">Levenshtein</span> <span class="p">{</span>

    <span class="kd">private</span> <span class="kd">class</span> <span class="nc">func</span> <span class="bp">min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">numbers</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">Int</span><span class="p">...)</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="nb">Int</span> <span class="p">{</span>
        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">numbers</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="bp">reduce</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">numbers</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">],</span> <span class="n">combine</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">{</span><span class="nv">$0</span> <span class="o">&lt;</span> <span class="nv">$1</span> <span class="p">?</span> <span class="nv">$0</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="nv">$1</span><span class="p">})</span>
    <span class="p">}</span>

    <span class="kd">class</span> <span class="nc">Array2D</span> <span class="p">{</span>
        <span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nv">cols</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nb">Int</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rows</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nb">Int</span>
        <span class="kd">var</span> <span class="nv">matrix</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="nb">Int</span><span class="p">]</span>

        <span class="kd">init</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">cols</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nb">Int</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rows</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nb">Int</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
            <span class="kc">self</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">cols</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">cols</span>
            <span class="kc">self</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">rows</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">rows</span>
            <span class="n">matrix</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nb">Array</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">count</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="n">cols</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">rows</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">repeatedValue</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="p">}</span>

        <span class="kd">subscript</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">col</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nb">Int</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">row</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nb">Int</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="nb">Int</span> <span class="p">{</span>
            <span class="kr">get</span> <span class="p">{</span>
                <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">matrix</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">cols</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="n">row</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">col</span><span class="p">]</span>
            <span class="p">}</span>
            <span class="kr">set</span> <span class="p">{</span>
                <span class="n">matrix</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">cols</span><span class="o">*</span><span class="n">row</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="n">col</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">newValue</span>
            <span class="p">}</span>
        <span class="p">}</span>

        <span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nf">colCount</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="nb">Int</span> <span class="p">{</span>
            <span class="k">return</span> <span class="kc">self</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">cols</span>
        <span class="p">}</span>

        <span class="kd">func</span> <span class="nf">rowCount</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="nb">Int</span> <span class="p">{</span>
            <span class="k">return</span> <span class="kc">self</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">rows</span>
        <span class="p">}</span>
    <span class="p">}</span>

    <span class="kd">class</span> <span class="nc">func</span> <span class="n">distanceBetween</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">aStr</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">String</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">and</span> <span class="n">bStr</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nb">String</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">-&gt;</span> <span class="nb">Int</span> <span class="p">{</span>
        <span class="kd">let</span> <span class="nv">a</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nb">Array</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">aStr</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">utf16</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="kd">let</span> <span class="nv">b</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="nb">Array</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">bStr</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">utf16</span><span class="p">)</span>

        <span class="kd">let</span> <span class="nv">dist</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">Array2D</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">cols</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">a</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="bp">count</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">rows</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">b</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="bp">count</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span>

        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="k">in</span> <span class="mf">1.</span><span class="p">..</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="bp">count</span> <span class="p">{</span>
            <span class="n">dist</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">i</span>
        <span class="p">}</span>

        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="k">in</span> <span class="mf">1.</span><span class="p">..</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="bp">count</span> <span class="p">{</span>
            <span class="n">dist</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">j</span>
        <span class="p">}</span>

        <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="k">in</span> <span class="mf">1.</span><span class="p">..</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="bp">count</span> <span class="p">{</span>
            <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="k">in</span> <span class="mf">1.</span><span class="p">..</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="bp">count</span> <span class="p">{</span>
                <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">a</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">==</span> <span class="n">b</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">{</span>
                    <span class="n">dist</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="n">dist</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span>  <span class="c1">// noop</span>
                <span class="p">}</span> <span class="k">else</span> <span class="p">{</span>
                    <span class="n">dist</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="p">=</span> <span class="bp">min</span><span class="p">(</span>
                        <span class="n">dist</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="c1">// deletion</span>
                        <span class="n">dist</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>  <span class="c1">// insertion</span>
                        <span class="n">dist</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span>  <span class="c1">// substitution</span>
                    <span class="p">)</span>
                <span class="p">}</span>
            <span class="p">}</span>
        <span class="p">}</span>

        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">dist</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="bp">count</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">b</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="bp">count</span><span class="p">]</span>
    <span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre>
      </div> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Turing">Turing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Turing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
%find the levenshtein distance%
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
% Isaac Bragg-Gardiner
function LD (s, t : string) : int
    % a couple variables
    var cell_above := 0
    var cell_left := 0
    var cell_diagonal := 0
    var cost := 0

    %lengths
    var n := length (s)
    var m := length (t)

    %if a string is zero
    if n = 0 then
        result m
    elsif m = 0 then
        result n
    else
    end if
    % make an array with both words
    var matrix : array 0 .. n, 0 .. m of int

    % initialize array to the length of each word
    for i : 0 .. n
        matrix (i, 0) := i
    end for

    for i : 0 .. m
        matrix (0, i) := i
    end for
    % calculate total changes
    for i : 1 .. n
        for j : 1 .. m

            if s (i) = t (j) then
cost := 0
            else
                cost := 1
            end if
            cell_above := matrix (i - 1, j) + 1
            cell_left := matrix (i, j - 1) + 1
            cell_diagonal := matrix (i - 1, j - 1) + cost
            var mini := min (cell_above, cell_left)
            matrix (i, j) := min (mini, cell_diagonal)
        end for
    end for
    result matrix (n, m)
end LD

put LD ("s", "t")
</pre>
      </div>

	<span class="k">ReDim</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">a</span> <span class="p">),</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">b</span> <span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">)</span>

	<span class="k">For</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="k">To</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">b</span> <span class="p">):</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="k">Next</span>
	
 <span class="c">' Actual calculation</span>
	<span class="k">For</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="k">To</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">a</span> <span class="p">)</span>

                        <span class="k">If</span> <span class="n">Mid</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Mid</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">Then</span> <span class="n">cost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="k">Else</span> <span class="n">cost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="k">End</span> <span class="k">If</span>
			
			<span class="c">' Since min() function is not a part of VBScript, we'll "emulate" it below</span>

      <h2><span id="Visual_Basic_for_Applications_(no_Damerau_extension)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Visual_Basic_for_Applications_.28no_Damerau_extension.29">Visual Basic for Applications (no Damerau extension)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Visual Basic for Applications (no Damerau extension)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>This version is identical to JavaScript and PHP implementations in this article. I had problems when I tried to use the other VBA implementation in this article, so I had to adopt the version below.</p> 
      <p>Application.WorksheetFunction.Min() method is Excel-specific. If you implement it with other VBA-enabled applications, uncomment the conditional block and comment out the Application.WorksheetFunction.Min() line.</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="k">Function</span> <span class="nf">levenshtein</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">a</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">String</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">b</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">String</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">Integer</span>

    <span class="k">Dim</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">Integer</span>
    <span class="k">Dim</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">Integer</span>
    <span class="k">Dim</span> <span class="n">cost</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">Integer</span>
    <span class="k">Dim</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="p">(,)</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">Integer</span>
    <span class="k">Dim</span> <span class="n">min1</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">Integer</span>
    <span class="k">Dim</span> <span class="n">min2</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">Integer</span>
    <span class="k">Dim</span> <span class="n">min3</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">Integer</span>
    
    <span class="k">If</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">a</span> <span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="k">Then</span>
        <span class="n">levenshtein</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">b</span> <span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="k">Exit</span> <span class="k">Function</span>
    <span class="nf">End</span> <span class="k">If</span>
    
    <span class="k">If</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">b</span> <span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="k">Then</span>
        <span class="n">levenshtein</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">a</span> <span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="k">Exit</span> <span class="k">Function</span>
    <span class="nf">End</span> <span class="k">If</span>
    
    <span class="k">ReDim</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="p">))</span>
    
    <span class="k">For</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="k">To</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="n">d</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">i</span>
    <span class="k">Next</span>
    
    <span class="k">For</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="k">To</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="n">d</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">j</span>
    <span class="k">Next</span>
    
    <span class="k">For</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="k">To</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="k">For</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="k">To</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="p">)</span>
            <span class="k">If</span> <span class="n">Mid</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Mid</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">Then</span>
                <span class="n">cost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
            <span class="k">Else</span>
                <span class="n">cost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span>
            <span class="k">End</span> <span class="k">If</span>
            
            <span class="c">' Since Min() function is not a part of VBA, we'll "emulate" it below</span>
            <span class="n">min1</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">d</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span>
            <span class="n">min2</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">d</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span>
            <span class="n">min3</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span><span class="n">d</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">cost</span><span class="p">)</span>
            
<span class="c">'            If min1 &lt;= min2 And min1 &lt;= min3 Then</span>
<span class="c">'                d(i, j) = min1</span>
<span class="c">'            ElseIf min2 &lt;= min1 And min2 &lt;= min3 Then</span>
<span class="c">'                d(i, j) = min2</span>
<span class="c">'            Else</span>
<span class="c">'                d(i, j) = min3</span>
<span class="c">'            End If</span>
            
            <span class="c">' In Excel we can use Min() function that is included</span>
            <span class="c">' as a method of WorksheetFunction object</span>
            <span class="n">d</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Application</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">WorksheetFunction</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="n">Min</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">min1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">min2</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">min3</span><span class="p">)</span>
        <span class="k">Next</span>
    <span class="k">Next</span>
    
    <span class="n">levenshtein</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">d</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">a</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">b</span><span class="p">))</span>

<span class="k">End</span> <span class="k">Function</span>
</pre>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="MapBasic">MapBasic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: MapBasic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>This version is identical to VB implementations in this article.</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>
<span class="n">type</span> <span class="n">twoDimArrayType</span>
 	<span class="n">secondArray</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="ow">as</span> <span class="kt">integer</span>
<span class="k">end</span> <span class="n">type</span>

<span class="k">Dim</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">Integer</span>
<span class="k">Dim</span> <span class="n">j</span> <span class="ow">As</span> <span class="kt">Integer</span>

<span class="c">'If one of the parameter is null, then the result will be the length of the other parameter...</span>
  <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">firstString</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="k">Then</span>
      <span class="n">calculateLevenshteinDistance</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">secondString</span><span class="p">)</span>
      <span class="k">exit</span> <span class="k">Function</span>
  <span class="nf">end</span> <span class="k">if</span>
  <span class="k">if</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">secondString</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="k">Then</span>
      <span class="n">calculateLevenshteinDistance</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">Len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">firstString</span><span class="p">)</span>
       <span class="k">exit</span> <span class="k">Function</span>
  <span class="nf">end</span> <span class="k">if</span>
  
<span class="c">'Initializing array...</span>
	<span class="k">redim</span> <span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">len</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">firstString</span><span class="p">)</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span>
	<span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">1</span> <span class="k">to</span> <span class="n">ubound</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">)</span>

	<span class="k">next</span>

<span class="c">'Deletion...</span>
  <span class="k">For</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="k">To</span> <span class="n">ubound</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">)</span>
      <span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">secondArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span>
  <span class="k">Next</span>
  
<span class="c">'Insertion ...</span>
  <span class="k">For</span> <span class="n">i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="k">To</span> <span class="n">ubound</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">ubound</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">)).</span><span class="n">secondArray</span><span class="p">)</span>
      <span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">secondArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span>
  <span class="k">Next</span>
	
<span class="c">'Actual calculation...	</span>
  <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">2</span> <span class="k">to</span> <span class="n">ubound</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">)</span>
  	<span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">2</span> <span class="k">to</span> <span class="n">ubound</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">secondArray</span><span class="p">)</span>	
    	<span class="k">If</span> <span class="n">StringCompare</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">Mid$</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">firstString</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">),</span> <span class="n">Mid$</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">secondString</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">))</span><span class="o">=</span><span class="mi">0</span>  <span class="k">Then</span>
      	<span class="n">cost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span>
      <span class="k">Else</span>
      	<span class="n">cost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">1</span>
      <span class="k">End</span> <span class="k">If</span>
			<span class="n">min1</span> <span class="o">=</span>  <span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">secondArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span> 
			<span class="n">min2</span> <span class="o">=</span>  <span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">secondArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span> 
			<span class="n">min3</span> <span class="o">=</span>  <span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">secondArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="n">cost</span>    
			<span class="k">If</span> <span class="n">min1</span> <span class="o">&lt;=</span> <span class="n">min2</span> <span class="ow">And</span> <span class="n">min1</span> <span class="o">&lt;=</span> <span class="n">min3</span> <span class="k">Then</span>

				<span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">secondArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">min2</span>
			<span class="k">Else</span>
				<span class="n">FirstArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">i</span><span class="p">).</span><span class="n">secondArray</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="n">j</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="n">min3</span>
			<span class="k">End</span> <span class="k">If</span>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Teslock">Teslock</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Teslock">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>This is the Levenshtein distance calculation in Teslock Machine Language.</p> 
      <pre>
.declare singlecall virtual LevenshteinDistance[args(2) string s1, string s2]: out unsigned int
 main
    (
    define unsigned int constant "cost_ins" == 1;
    define unsigned int constant "cost_del" == 1;
    define unsigned int constant "cost_sub" == 1;

    define unsigned int variable "n1" == calculate::string_operations&gt;length("s1");
    define unsigned int variable "n2" == calculate::string_operations&gt;length("s2");

    define unsigned int_array(calculate::string_operations&gt;array_instantiation("p")&gt;fixed_length("n2", ++1));
    define unsigned int_array(calculate::string_operations&gt;array_instantiation("q")&gt;fixed_length("n2", ++1));
    define unsigned int_array(calculate::string_operations&gt;array_instantiation("r")&gt;variable_length);

    p&gt;array_vector&gt;0 == 0;
    loop_for&gt;finalized(define unsigned int variable "j" == 1)&gt;break_condition("j" &lt;= "n2")&gt;forward_condition(++j)
    (
        p&gt;array_vector&gt;j == p&gt;array_vector&gt;j::access&gt;+constants::cost_ins;
    )

    q&gt;array_vector&gt;0 == 0;
    loop_for&gt;finalized(define unsigned int variable "i" == 1)&gt;break_condition("i" &lt;= "n1")&gt;forward_condition(++i)
    (
        q&gt;array_vector&gt;0 == p&gt;array_vector&gt;0::access&gt;+constants::cost_del;
        
        loop for&gt;finalized(define unsigned int variable "j" == 1)&gt;break_condition("j" &lt;= "n2")&gt;forward_condition(++j)
        (
            define unsigned int variable "d_del" == p&gt;array_vector&gt;j::access&gt;+constants::cost_del;
            define unsigned int variable "d_ins" == q&gt;array_vector&gt;j[delegate_handle::j::access&gt;-1]&gt;+constants::cost_ins;
            define unsigned int veriable "d_sub" == p&gt;array_vector&gt;j[delegate_handle::j::access&gt;-1]&gt;+logical_operations&gt;xor_result["s1"::access&gt;"s1"[delegate_handle::j::access&gt;-1]?0&gt;return_handle_as_result constants::"cost_sub"];
            q&gt;array_vector&gt;j == dll_extern::math_interop_singlecall(min)::[args(3) (d_del, d_ins), d_sub;
        )
        local&gt;"r" == "p"(self_typecast::ignore_unsafe_condition);
        local&gt;"p" == "q"(self_typecast);
        local&gt;"q" == "r"(self_typecast);    
    )
    
    logical_result(param p::singlecall)::define&gt;"return" == p&gt;array_vector&gt;"n2";
)

</pre> 
      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abap">Abap</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Algorithm_Implementation/Strings/Levenshtein_distance&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Abap">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>Please note that there is a standard ABAP function <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://help.sap.com/abapdocu_702/en/abendistance_functions.htm">distance</a> which calculates the Levenshtein distance without need for the below coding.</p> 
      <div class="mw-highlight mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr"> 
       <pre>

               <span class="k">RETURNING</span> <span class="k">value</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nv">r</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="k">TYPE </span><span class="nv">i</span><span class="p">.</span>

    <span class="k">DEFINE</span> <span class="nv">m_get</span><span class="p">.</span>
      <span class="nv">l_m_index</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">(</span> <span class="p">(</span> <span class="nv">l_l_t</span> <span class="o">*</span> <span class="p">(</span> <span class="nv">l_m_i</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">&amp;2</span> <span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="nv">l_m_j</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="p">(</span> <span class="n">&amp;1</span> <span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="mi">1</span> <span class="p">.</span>
      <span class="k">read</span> <span class="k">table</span> <span class="nv">l_d</span> <span class="k">into</span> <span class="nv">r</span> <span class="k">index</span> <span class="nv">l_m_index</span><span class="p">.</span>
      <span class="k">add</span> <span class="n">&amp;3</span> <span class="k">to</span> <span class="nv">r</span><span class="p">.</span>
