    <span class="k">END-OF-DEFINITION</span><span class="p">.</span>
    <span class="k">DATA</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nv">l_d</span>       <span class="k">TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF</span> <span class="nv">i</span><span class="p">,</span>
          <span class="nv">l_v</span>       <span class="k">TYPE SORTED TABLE OF</span> <span class="nv">i</span> <span class="k">WITH UNIQUE KEY</span> <span class="nv">table_line</span><span class="p">,</span>
          <span class="nv">l_cost</span>    <span class="k">TYPE </span><span class="nv">i</span><span class="p">,</span>
          <span class="nv">l_m_i</span>     <span class="k">TYPE </span><span class="nv">i</span><span class="p">,</span>

          <span class="nv">l_l_s</span>     <span class="k">TYPE </span><span class="nv">i</span><span class="p">,</span>
          <span class="nv">l_l_t</span>     <span class="k">TYPE </span><span class="nv">i</span><span class="p">.</span>

    <span class="nv">l_l_s</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nv">STRLEN</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="nv">i_s</span> <span class="p">).</span>
    <span class="nv">l_l_t</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nv">STRLEN</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="nv">i_t</span> <span class="p">).</span>

    <span class="k">DO</span> <span class="nv">l_l_s</span> <span class="k">TIMES</span><span class="p">.</span>
      <span class="nv">l_m_i</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nv">sy</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="nv">index</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">.</span>

      <span class="k">DO</span> <span class="nv">l_l_t</span> <span class="k">TIMES</span><span class="p">.</span> <span class="c1">"#EC CI_NESTED</span>
        <span class="nv">l_m_j</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nv">sy</span><span class="o">-</span><span class="nv">index</span> <span class="o">-</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">.</span>

          <span class="k">IF</span> <span class="nv">i_s</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="nv">l_m_i</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nv">i_t</span><span class="o">+</span><span class="nv">l_m_j</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">).</span>
            <span class="nv">l_cost</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">.</span>

          <span class="k">ENDIF</span><span class="p">.</span>

        <span class="k">ELSE</span><span class="p">.</span>

          <span class="k">CLEAR</span> <span class="nv">l_v</span><span class="p">.</span>
          <span class="nv">m_get</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span>  <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="mi">0</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span> <span class="o">-</span><span class="mi">1</span> <span class="nv">l_cost</span><span class="p">.</span>
          <span class="k">READ</span> <span class="k">TABLE</span> <span class="nv">l_v</span> <span class="k">INTO</span> <span class="nv">r</span> <span class="k">INDEX</span> <span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">.</span>
        <span class="k">ENDIF</span><span class="p">.</span>
        <span class="k">APPEND</span> <span class="nv">r</span> <span class="k">TO</span> <span class="nv">l_d</span><span class="p">.</span>

      <span class="k">ENDDO</span><span class="p">.</span>
    <span class="k">ENDDO</span><span class="p">.</span>
  <span class="k">ENDMETHOD</span><span class="p">.</span>                    <span class="c1">"distance</span>
<span class="k">ENDCLASS</span><span class="p">.</span>                    <span class="c1">"lcl_levenshtein IMPLEMENTATION</span>

<span class="k">START-OF-SELECTION</span><span class="p">.</span>
  <span class="k">DATA</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="nv">d</span> <span class="k">TYPE </span><span class="nv">i</span><span class="p">.</span>

  <span class="nv">d</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nv">lcl_levenshtein</span><span class="o">=&gt;</span><span class="nf">distance</span><span class="p">(</span> <span class="nv">i_s</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'sitting'</span> <span class="nv">i_t</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="s1">'kitten'</span> <span class="p">).</span>
  <span class="k">WRITE</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="p">/</span> <span class="nv">d</span><span class="p">.</span>
</pre>
      </div>
